local function decode(data)
  local b='ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/='
  data = data:gsub('[^'..b..']','')
  return (data:gsub('.', function(x)
    if x=='=' then return '' end
    local r,f='',(b:find(x)-1)
    for i=6,1,-1 do r=r..(f%2^i - f%2^(i-1)>0 and '1' or '0') end
    return r
  end):gsub('%d%d%d?%d?%d?%d?%d?%d?',function(x)
    if #x~=8 then return '' end
    local c=0
    for i=1,8 do c=c+(x:sub(i,i)=='1' and 2^(8-i) or 0) end
    return string.char(c)
  end))
end

if not loadstring or not getfenv or not debug then error("Runtime Error") end
if debug.getinfo(1).what ~= "Lua" then error("VM Tampered") end
for i=1,3 do pcall(function() debug.getlocal(1,i) end) end
for i=1,2 do pcall(function() debug.getupvalue(function() end,i) end) end
if type(__payload)~="string" then error("Payload Tampered") end
if md5(__payload)~="2a31b074eb345641480433c7aa7924d4" then error("Payload Checksum Failed") end


local function exec(code)
  local f, err = loadstring(code)
  if not f then error("Execution Error: "..(err or "?")) end
  return f()
end
exec(decode(__payload))
